<td style="width:11%;vertical-align:top" align="left"><span style="font-weight:bold">Item&#8201;1.01.</span></td>
<td align="left" style="vertical-align:top"> <p style=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;text-align:left">Entry into a Material Definitive Agreement. </p></td></tr></table> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#8194;On May&#160;31, 2024, StepStone Group Inc., a Delaware corporation (the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration:underline">Company</span>&#8221;) and StepStone Group LP, a Delaware limited partnership (the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration:underline">Partnership</span>&#8221;), completed the first annual exchange (the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration:underline">2024 Exchange</span>&#8221;) as part of the previously announced transactions to acquire equity interests of StepStone Group Real Estate LP, a Delaware limited partnership (&#8220;<span style="text-decoration:underline">SRE</span>&#8221;), StepStone Group Real Assets LP, a Delaware limited partnership (&#8220;<span style="text-decoration:underline">SIRA</span>&#8221;) and StepStone Group Private Debt AG (formerly known as Swiss Capital Alternative Investments AG), a private company limited by shares incorporated in the canton of Zurich (&#8220;<span style="text-decoration:underline">SPD</span>&#8221;, and collectively with SRE and SIRA, the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration:underline">Asset Class</span><span style="text-decoration:underline"></span><span style="text-decoration:underline">&#160;Entities</span>&#8221;, and each, an &#8220;<span style="text-decoration:underline">Asset Class</span><span style="text-decoration:underline"></span><span style="text-decoration:underline">&#160;Entity</span>&#8221;) pursuant to (i)&#160;the Transaction Agreement (the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration:underline">SRE Transaction Agreement</span>&#8221;), dated as of February&#160;7, 2024, with SRE, Jeffrey Giller, solely in his capacity as seller representative, and the seller parties signatory thereto (the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration:underline">SRE Sellers</span>&#8221;), (ii)&#160;the Transaction Agreement (the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration:underline">SIRA Transaction Agreement</span>&#8221;), dated as of February&#160;7, 2024, with SIRA, James O&#8217;Leary, solely in his capacity as seller representative, and the seller parties signatory thereto (the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration:underline">SIRA Sellers</span>&#8221;), and (iii)&#160;the Transaction Agreement (the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration:underline">SPD Transaction Agreement</span>&#8221;, and collectively with the SRE Tranaction Agreement and the SIRA Transaction Agreement, the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration:underline">Transaction Agreements</span>&#8221;), dated as of February&#160;7, 2024, with StepStone Europe Limited, a private limited liability company incorporated in England and a wholly-owned subsidiary of the Company, SPD, Marcel Schindler, solely in his capacity as seller representative, and SC Partner LP, a Cayman Islands exempted limited partnership (the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration:underline">SPD Seller</span>&#8221;, and collectively with the SRE Sellers and the SIRA Sellers, the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration:underline">Sellers</span>&#8221;, and each, a &#8220;<span style="text-decoration:underline">Seller</span>&#8221;), respectively. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#8194;The portion of the equity interests acquired in the 2024 Exchange was approximately 5% of each Asset Class&#160;Entity. As a result of the 2024 Exchange, the Partnership now owns approximately 56% of the outstanding equity interests of SRE, 54% of the outstanding equity interests of SIRA and 55% of the outstanding equity interests of SPD. The amount of consideration delivered was calculated using exchange ratios based on a formula establishing an assumed value of each Asset Class&#160;Entity based on its estimated adjusted net income, relative to an adjusted trading multiple for the Company&#8217;s Class&#160;A Common Stock, par value $0.001 per share (the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration:underline">Class</span><span style="text-decoration:underline"></span><span style="text-decoration:underline">&#160;A Common Stock</span>&#8221;), relative to the Company&#8217;s estimated adjusted net income. The aggregate consideration paid by the Company and the Partnership in the 2024 Exchange was approximately (i) $13&#160;million in cash, (ii)&#160;513,394 shares of Class&#160;A Common Stock, and (iii) 2,239,185 Class&#160;D Units of the Partnership (the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration:underline">Class</span><span style="text-decoration:underline"></span><span style="text-decoration:underline">&#160;D Units</span>&#8221;). </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold"><span style="font-style:italic">Tenth Amended&#160;&amp; Restated Limited Partnership Agreement </span></p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#8194;In connection with the transactions contemplated by the SRE Transaction Agreement and SIRA Transaction Agreement, the Partnership entered into a Tenth Amended&#160;&amp; Restated Limited Partnership Agreement of StepStone Partnership LP (the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration:underline">A&amp;R Partnership Agreement</span>&#8221;) at the closing of the 2024 Exchange on May&#160;31, 2024. The A&amp;R Partnership Agreement creates Class&#160;D Units of the Partnership (the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration:underline">Class</span><span style="text-decoration:underline"></span><span style="text-decoration:underline">&#160;D Units</span>&#8221;) to be issued to the Sellers under the SRE Transaction Agreement and SIRA Transaction Agreement. The rights and obligations applicable to holders of the Class&#160;D Units are substantially the same as those applicable to existing holders of Class&#160;C Units of the Partnership under the Ninth Amended&#160;&amp; Restated Limited Partnership Agreement of the Partnership. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#8194;The foregoing summary does not purport to be a complete description and is qualified in its entirety by reference to the full text of the A&amp;R Partnership Agreement, which is attached hereto as Exhibit 10.1 and is incorporated herein by reference </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold"><span style="font-style:italic">Second Amended and Restated Registration Rights Agreement </span></p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#8194;In connection with the transactions contemplated by the Transaction Agreements, the Company entered into a Second Amended and Restated Registration Rights Agreement (the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration:underline">Second A&amp;R RRA</span>&#8221;) at the closing of the 2024 Exchange on May&#160;31, 2024, on substially the same terms as the existing Amended and Restated Registration Rights Agreement, dated as of September&#160;20, 2021. The Second A&amp;R RRA grants customary registration rights to the Sellers, including demand registration rights, shelf registration rights and piggback registration rights. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#8194;The foregoing summary does not purport to be a complete description and is qualified in its entirety by reference to the full text of the Second A&amp;R RRA, which is attached hereto as Exhibit 10.2 and is incorporated herein by reference. </p>
</div></div>



<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<hr style="color:#999999;height:3px;width:100%"/>

<div style="text-align:center"><div style="width:8.5in;text-align:left;margin-left: auto;margin-right: auto">
 <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold"><span style="font-style:italic">Class&#160;D Exchange Agreement </span></p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#8194;In connection with the transactions contemplated by the SRE Transaction Agreement and SIRA Transaction Agreement, the Company entered into a Class&#160;D Exchange Agreement (the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration:underline">Class&#160;D Exchange Agreement</span>&#8221;) at the closing of the 2024 Exchange on May&#160;31, 2024. The Class&#160;D Exchange Agreement provides, among other things, Sellers under the SRE Transaction Agreement and SIRA Transaction Agreement with the ability, in certain circumstances and subject to certain conditions, to exchange the Class&#160;D Units issued to them in connection with the SRE Transaction Agreement and SIRA Transaction Agreement on a one for one basis with shares of Class&#160;A Common Stock of the Company, par value $0.001 (the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration:underline">Class&#160;A Common Stock</span>&#8221;). In addition, the Class&#160;D Exchange Agreement restricts the exchange of the Class&#160;D Units issued to such Sellers, which restriction shall apply for a maximum of one year (or two years if a Transaction Agreement Exchange (as defined in the Class&#160;D Exchange Agreement) constitutes an Acceleration Exchange (as defined in the Class&#160;D Exchange Agreement)), subject to certain exceptions. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#8194;The foregoing summary does not purport to be a complete description and is qualified in its entirety by reference to the full text of the Class&#160;D Exchange Agreement, which is attached hereto as Exhibit 10.3 and is incorporated herein by reference. </p> <p style="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p>
<table style="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;border:0;width:100%" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">

One share of Class&#160;A Common Stock will be issuable upon exchange of each Class&#160;D Unit and such issuances will be made in reliance upon the exemption set forth in Sections 3(a)(9) and/or 4(a)(2) under the Securities Act. </p> <p style="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>TENTH AMENDED AND RESTATED </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>LIMITED PARTNERSHIP AGREEMENT </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><SMALL>OF</SMALL> </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>STEPSTONE
GROUP LP </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><B>TENTH AMENDED AND RESTATED LIMITED PARTNERSHIP AGREEMENT</B> (the &#147;<B>Agreement</B>&#148;) of
StepStone Group LP, a Delaware limited partnership (the &#147;<B>Partnership</B>&#148;), is made and entered into as of May&nbsp;31, 2024, by and between StepStone Group Holdings LLC, as General Partner, and each of the persons admitted as a Limited
Partner as of the date hereof or admitted from time to time after the date hereof as a Limited Partner in accordance with the terms of this Agreement (collectively, the &#147;<B>Partners</B>&#148; with each being referred to separately as a
&#147;<B>Partner</B>&#148;). </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">WHEREAS, since September&nbsp;20, 2021, the Partnership has been governed by the Ninth
Amended and Restated Agreement of Limited Partnership of the Partnership (the &#147;<B>Ninth Amended and Restated Agreement</B>&#148;); and </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">WHEREAS, the General Partner desires to amend the Ninth Amended and Restated Agreement primarily to establish a new class of
Units and to amend and restate the Ninth Amended and Restated Agreement to include such amendments and to read in its entirety as set forth herein. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">NOW, THEREFORE, in consideration of the mutual covenants contained herein and for other good and valuable consideration, the
Partners hereby agree (and each Person who subsequently shall become a Partner shall agree) as follows: </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>ARTICLE 1 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>ORGANIZATIONAL MATTERS </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">1.1&#8195;<U>Name</U>. The name of the Partnership is StepStone Group LP. The Partnership may also conduct business at the
same time under one or more fictitious names if the General Partner determines that such is in the best interests of the Partnership. The General Partner may change the name of the Partnership, from time to time, in accordance with applicable Law.
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">1.2&#8195;<U>Principal Place of Business; Other Places of Business</U>. The principal place of business of the
Partnership is located at 4225&nbsp;Executive Square, Suite&nbsp;1600, La Jolla, CA&nbsp;92037 or such other place within or outside the State of Delaware as the General Partner may from time to time designate. The Partnership may maintain offices
and places of business at such other place or places within or outside the State of Delaware as the General Partner deems advisable. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">1.3&#8195;<U>Business Purpose</U>. The principal purpose of the Partnership is to engage in the business of providing private
market and other alternative investment advisory services and engaging in and managing related investment activities. The Partnership may also engage in any and all lawful business, purpose or activity in which a limited partnership may be engaged
under </P>
</DIV></Center>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">
applicable Law (including, without limitation, the Act) as may be determined by the General Partner from time to time. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">1.4&#8195;<U>Amendments to Certificate and Other Filings</U>. The General Partner may execute and file any duly authorized
amendments to the Certificate of Limited Partnership of the Partnership from time to time in a form prescribed by the Act. The General Partner shall also cause to be made, on behalf of the Partnership, such additional filings and recordings as the
General Partner shall deem necessary or advisable. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">1.5&#8195;<U>Designated Agent for Service of Process</U>. The address
of the registered office of the Partnership in the State of Delaware, and the name and address of the registered agent of the Partnership for service of process on the Partnership in the State of Delaware, is The Corporation Trust Company,
Corporation Trust Center, 1209 Orange Street, Wilmington, New Castle County, Delaware, 19801. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">1.6&#8195;<U>Term</U>. The
Partnership shall continue until terminated pursuant to this Agreement. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">1.7&#8195;<U>Rights</U>. The rights and
liabilities of the Partners of the Partnership shall be as provided in the Act, except as otherwise expressly provided herein. In the event of any inconsistency between any terms and conditions contained in this Agreement and any <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-mandatory</FONT> provisions of the Act, the terms and conditions contained in this Agreement shall govern. The Partnership has been established as a series limited partnership pursuant to
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">&#167;17-218</FONT> of the Act but no such series have been or, in the absence of a properly adopted amendment to this Agreement, will be, issued. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>ARTICLE 2 </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>DEFINITIONS
</B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">Capitalized words and phrases used and not otherwise defined elsewhere in this Agreement shall have the following
meanings: </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">2.1&#8195;&#147;<B>2019 Dilutable Units</B>&#148; means Units outstanding immediately after the 2019 Equity
Transaction, other than the Class&nbsp;B2 Units and Units acquired by 2019 Equity Investors pursuant to the 2019 Equity Transaction. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">2.2&#8195;&#147;<B>2019 Equity Investors</B>&#148; means the purchasers of Units in the 2019 Equity Transaction. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">2.3&#8195;&#147;<B>2019 Equity Transaction</B>&#148; means the purchases and sales of Units that occurred on August&nbsp;19,
2019. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">2.4&#8195;&#147;<B>2019 Redeemed Partners</B>&#148; means the Limited Partners whose Units were redeemed in the
2019 Equity Transaction. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">2.5&#8195;&#147;<B>2021</B> <B>Transaction Agreement</B>&#148; means that certain Transaction
Agreement, dated as of July&nbsp;7, 2021, by and among the Partnership, SSG, certain holders of Class&nbsp;C Units and certain other parties as set forth therein. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">2 </P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">2.6&#8195;&#147;<B>2022 Option Agreement</B>&#148; means that certain Option

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">2.7&#8195;&#147;<B>2024 Transaction Agreements</B>&#148; means collectively (i)&nbsp;that certain Transaction Agreement, dated

dated as of February&nbsp;7, 2024, by and among SSG, the Partnership, StepStone Group Real Assets LP, James O&#146;Leary, solely in his capacity as a seller representative, and the seller parties signatory thereto and (iii)&nbsp;that certain

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">2.8&#8195;&#147;<B>Act</B>&#148; means the Delaware Revised Uniform Limited Partnership Act, as amended from time to time.
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">2.9&#8195;&#147;<B>Active Partner</B>&#148; means a Class&nbsp;B Limited Partner or Class&nbsp;B2 Limited Partner
employed by the SSG Group or actively engaged in a service provider capacity in the business or management of the SSG Group, for so long as there has not been a Termination Event with respect to such Limited Partner; <I>provided</I> that, for the
avoidance of doubt none of (i)&nbsp;Argonaut Holdings, LLC, (ii)&nbsp;Sanford Energy, Inc., (iii) Davis Investment Holdings, LLC, (iv)&nbsp;ALD 2020 GST Trust or (v)&nbsp;any holder of Partnership Interests that is owned by an advisory fund or
account advised or <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-advised</FONT> by Davis Investment Holdings, LLC or one of its Affiliates shall be deemed Active Partners. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">2.10&#8195;&#147;<B>Additional Limited Partners</B>&#148; means those Persons admitted to the Partnership pursuant to
<U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;3.4</U>. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">2.11&#8195;&#147;<B>Adjusted Capital Account Deficit</B>&#148; means, with respect
to any Partner, the deficit balance, if any, in such Partner&#146;s Capital Account as of the end of the relevant fiscal period, after giving effect to the following adjustments: </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:11%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">2.11.1&#8195;Add to such Capital Account the following items: </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:5%; text-indent:12%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">&#8194;(a)&#8195;The amount, if any, that such Partner is obligated to contribute to the Partnership upon
liquidation of such Partner&#146;s Interest; and </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:5%; text-indent:12%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">&#8194;(b)&#8195;The amount that such Partner is
obligated to restore or is deemed to be obligated to restore pursuant to Treas. Reg. &#167; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">1.704-1(b)(2)(ii)(</FONT><I>c</I>) or the penultimate sentence of each of Treas. Reg. &#167;&#167; <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">1.704-2(g)(1)</FONT> and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">1.704-2(i)(5);</FONT> and </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:11%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">2.11.2&#8195;Subtract from such Capital Account such Partner&#146;s share of the items described in Treas. <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Reg.&nbsp;&#167;&#167;&nbsp;1.704-1(b)(2)(ii)(</FONT><I>d</I>)(<I>4</I>), (<I>5</I>) and (<I>6</I>). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">The foregoing definition of Adjusted Capital Account Deficit is intended to comply with the provisions of Treas. <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Reg.&nbsp;&#167;&nbsp;1.704-1(b)(2)(ii)(</FONT><I>d</I>) and shall be interpreted consistently therewith. </P>

</DIV></Center>

Active Partner, any event the result of which is that such Limited Partner&#146;s status as an Active Partner is Terminated for any reason. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">2.13&#8195;&#147;<B>Adjustment Percentage</B>&#148; is defined in <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;7.10.1</U>. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">2.14&#8195;&#147;<B>Admission Agreement</B>&#148; means, with respect to any Limited Partner, the purchase, subscription or

Person, any other Person that, directly or indirectly, through one or more intermediaries, controls, is controlled by, or is under common control with, the specified Person. For purposes of this definition, the term &#147;control&#148; (including
with correlative meanings, the terms &#147;controlling&#148;, &#147;controlled by&#148;, and &#147;under common control with&#148;), with respect to any Person, means the possession, directly or indirectly, of the power to direct or cause the
direction of the management and policies of such Person, either through the ownership of a majority of such Person&#146;s voting stock, by contract or otherwise. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">2.17&#8195;&#147;<B>Agreement</B>&#148; is defined in the Preamble and shall include any Class&nbsp;Designation, which shall
be an integral part of this Agreement. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">2.18&#8195;&#147;<B>Anti-Dilution Trigger</B>&#148; is defined in

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">2.24&#8195;&#147;<B>Base Percentage Interest</B>&#148; means, with respect to any Partner as of any date of determination, the
fraction (expressed as a percentage), the numerator of which is the number of Units held by such Partner and the denominator of which is the number of Units held by all Partners. For purposes of this calculation, the Unvested Class&nbsp;B2 Units of
any Class&nbsp;B2 Limited Partner shall be excluded (from both the numerator and the denominator). </P>

in Rule <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">13d-3</FONT> promulgated under the Exchange Act. </P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">2.30&#8195;&#147;<B>Cause</B>&#148; means, with respect to any Active Partner or, with respect to Section&nbsp;7.8.2(e) only,
any Class&nbsp;C Limited Partner or any Class&nbsp;D Limited Partner, that such Limited Partner commits any of the following acts and fails to cure said breach, if it is in fact curable, within thirty (30)&nbsp;days after written notice from the
General Partner of said breach: (a)&nbsp;conviction of, or plea of guilty or nolo contendere to, any criminal act involving moral turpitude, including, without limitation, fraud, embezzlement or misappropriation of funds or property;
(b)&nbsp;commission of a material act of dishonesty, fraud or misrepresentation which would reasonably be expected to adversely and materially affect the assets, business or prospects of the SSG Group; (c)&nbsp;willful breach of duty in the course
of providing services as an Active Partner; (d)&nbsp;material breach of this Agreement; and/or (e)&nbsp;materially failing to satisfy, perform or comply with any obligations, duties or undertakings that a Limited Partner owes to the SSG Group. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">2.31&#8195;&#147;<B>Change of Control</B>&#148; means: (i)&nbsp;an acquisition by any Person or group of Persons of Equity
Securities of the Partnership (other than the Ownership Group, the SSG Group or a member of either of them), whether already outstanding or&nbsp;newly issued, in a transaction or series of transactions, if immediately thereafter such Person or group
of Persons (other than the Ownership Group, the SSG Group or&nbsp;a member of either of them) has, or would have, directly or indirectly, Beneficial Ownership of fifty percent (50%) or more of the combined Equity Securities of the Partnership;
(ii)&nbsp;the sale of all or&nbsp;substantially all of the assets of the Partnership and its Subsidiaries, taken as a whole, directly or indirectly, to any Person or group of Persons (other than the Ownership Group, the SSG Group or a member of
either of them) in a transaction or&nbsp;series of transactions; or (iii)&nbsp;the consummation of a tender offer, merger, recapitalization, consolidation, business combination, reorganization or other transaction, or series of related transactions,
involving the Partnership and any other Person or group of Persons (other than the Ownership Group, the SSG Group or a member of either of them); unless, in the case of clause (ii)&nbsp;or&nbsp;(iii)&nbsp;of this definition, either
(1)&nbsp;then-existing Partners, immediately prior to such transaction or the first transaction in such series of transactions, will beneficially own more than fifty percent (50%) of the combined Equity Securities of the Partnership (or, if the
Partnership will not be the surviving entity in such transaction or series of transactions, such surviving entity) immediately after such transaction or series of transactions or (2)&nbsp;Persons who are Partners immediately prior
to&nbsp;such&nbsp;transaction or the first transaction in such series of transactions will be entitled to cast at least a majority of the votes </P>

respect to any Class&nbsp;B2 Units, the date on which all of the Class&nbsp;B2 Units issued to a Class&nbsp;B2 Limited Partner in an Admission Agreement become fully vested in accordance with the terms set forth in

LLC, a Delaware limited liability company, or any other Person that becomes a successor or an additional general partner of the Partnership as provided in this Agreement, in each such Person&#146;s capacity as general partner, in each case as the
context requires. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">2.65&#8195;&#147;<B>Gross Asset Value</B>&#148; means, with respect to any asset, the asset&#146;s
adjusted basis for federal income tax purposes, except as follows: </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:11%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">2.65.1&#8195;The initial Gross Asset Value of any
asset (other than money) contributed by a Partner to the Partnership shall be the gross fair market value of such asset. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:11%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">2.65.2&#8195;The Gross Asset Values of all assets shall be adjusted to equal their respective gross fair market values as
determined by the General Partner as of the following times: </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:5%; text-indent:12%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">&#8194;(a)&#8195;the acquisition of an
additional interest in the Partnership (other than in connection with the execution of this Agreement) by a new or existing Partner in exchange for more than a <I>de minimis</I> Capital Contribution, if the General Partner reasonably determines that
such adjustment is necessary or appropriate to reflect the relative economic interests of the Partners in the Partnership; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:5%; text-indent:12%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">&#8194;(b)&#8195;the distribution by the Partnership to a Partner of more than a <I>de minimis</I> amount of
Partnership assets as consideration for an interest in the Partnership, if the General Partner reasonably determines that such adjustment is necessary or appropriate to reflect the relative economic interests of the Partners in the Partnership; </P>

 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">8 </P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:11%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">2.65.3&#8195;The Gross Asset Value of any Partnership asset distributed to a Partner shall be the gross fair market value
of&nbsp;such asset on the date of distribution, as determined by the General Partner. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:11%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">2.65.4&#8195;The Gross Asset

<U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;2.64.4</U> to the extent that the General Partner reasonably determines that an adjustment pursuant to <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;2.64.2</U> above is necessary or appropriate in connection with a transaction that
would otherwise result in an adjustment pursuant to this <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;2.64.4</U>. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:11%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">2.65.5&#8195;If the

Partner is an Active Partner for the entirety of such period, without proration. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>ARTICLE 3 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>CAPITAL; CAPITAL ACCOUNTS AND PARTNERS </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">3.1&#8195;<U>Capital Contributions</U>. Except as expressly provided herein with respect to SSG or in the Class&nbsp;B
Exchange Agreement, (i)&nbsp;no Partner shall be required to make any Capital Contributions to the Partnership without such Partner&#146;s consent and (ii)&nbsp;no Partner shall be permitted to make any Capital Contributions to the Partnership
without the General Partner&#146;s consent. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">3.2&#8195;<U>Capital Accounts</U>. A Capital Account shall be established and
maintained for each Partner in accordance with Treas. Reg. &#167; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">1.704-1(b)(2)(iv)</FONT> (a &#147;<B>Capital Account</B>&#148;). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">3.3&#8195;<U>Classes of Units</U>. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">3.3.1&#8195;Upon effectiveness of this Agreement, the Interests of Limited Partners are represented by units of Partnership
Interest (&#147;<B>Units</B>&#148;), which are divided into: </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:5%; text-indent:11%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">(a)&#8195;Class A Units (the
&#147;<B>Class</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;A Units</B>&#148;), which are issuable to SSG and such other Persons as the General Partner shall determine; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:5%; text-indent:11%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">(b)&#8195;Class B Units (the &#147;<B>Class</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;B Units</B>&#148;), which shall be issued only
(x)&nbsp;in accordance with <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;3.3.4</U>, and (y)&nbsp;with respect to and upon full vesting of Class&nbsp;B2 Units; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:5%; text-indent:11%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">(c)&#8195;Class B2 Units (the &#147;<B>Class</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;B2 Units</B>&#148;), none of which shall be
issued after the date hereof; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:5%; text-indent:11%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">(d)&#8195;Class C Units (the &#147;<B>Class</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;C
Units</B>&#148;), which have been issued as consideration to certain of the Sellers (as defined in the 2021 Transaction Agreement) pursuant to the 2021 Transaction Agreement and shall be issued only in accordance with
<U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;3.3.4</U>; and </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:5%; text-indent:11%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">(e)&#8195;Class D Units (the
&#147;<B>Class</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;D Units</B>&#148;), which shall be issued as consideration (i)&nbsp;to the Sellers (as defined in the 2024 Transaction Agreements) pursuant to certain of the 2024 Transaction Agreements and (ii)&nbsp;pursuant to the
2022 Option Agreement, in each case, only in accordance with <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;3.3.4</U>. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">15 </P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">3.3.2&#8195;The General Partner is authorized to establish and designate
additional classes and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-classes</FONT> of Units, including preferred Units that rank senior to any then-existing Units and any other new class of Units whose rights, obligations, terms and conditions are set forth
on a Class&nbsp;Designation. The General Partner may establish and determine the designations, priorities, powers, preferences, limitations and relative rights of any additional class or classes of Partnership Interests. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">3.3.3&#8195;The Partnership may issue additional Units in exchange for cash or other consideration, including additional
classes of Units, to such Persons, at such times, and having such terms as the General Partner may determine in accordance with this Agreement. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">3.3.4&#8195;<U>Units and Capital Stock of SSG</U>. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:5%; text-indent:11%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">(a)&#8195;Each Class&nbsp;B Unit shall be associated with and stapled to one share of Class&nbsp;B Common
Stock. Upon any issuance of Class&nbsp;B Units, each Limited Partner receiving such Units shall purchase from SSG, concurrently with the issuance of Class&nbsp;B Units, one share of Class&nbsp;B Common Stock for the consideration of the par value
thereof. Upon any surrender, redemption or conversion of any such Class&nbsp;B Unit, the holder thereof shall concurrently surrender to SSG or the Partnership (as applicable) the associated share of Class&nbsp;B Common Stock in exchange for payment
by SSG or the Partnership (as applicable) of the par value thereof. Without the specific approval of the General Partner, no Transfer of a Class&nbsp;B Unit shall be effected without a simultaneous Transfer of the corresponding share of Class&nbsp;B
Common Stock. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:5%; text-indent:11%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">(b)&#8195;Class&nbsp;A Units may be issued only in accordance with <U>Sections
3.3.4(c)</U> and <U>(f)</U>&nbsp;and no additional Class&nbsp;B Units, Class&nbsp;B2 Units or Class&nbsp;C Units may be issued by the Partnership except in accordance with <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;3.3.4(f)</U> below. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:5%; text-indent:11%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">(c)&#8195;If SSG issues shares of Class&nbsp;A Common Stock (other than an issuance pursuant to the
Class&nbsp;B Exchange Agreement, the Class&nbsp;C Exchange Agreement or the Class&nbsp;D Exchange Agreement), unless such net proceeds are used to purchase Units from Limited Partners, SSG shall promptly contribute to the Partnership all the net
proceeds and property (if any) received by SSG with respect to such Class&nbsp;A Common Stock. Upon the contribution by SSG to the Partnership of all (but not less than all) of such net proceeds and property (if any) so received by SSG, the General
Partner shall cause the Partnership to issue a number of Class&nbsp;A Units equal to the number of shares of Class&nbsp;A Common Stock so issued, registered in the name of SSG, such that, at all times, the number of Class&nbsp;A Units held by SSG
equals the number of outstanding shares of Class&nbsp;A Common Stock. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:5%; text-indent:11%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">(d)&#8195;It is the intent that
each unit of Capital Stock be generally equivalent in economic respects to an Equivalent Unit. Accordingly, if SSG issues shares of Capital Stock other than Class&nbsp;A Common Stock, SSG shall promptly contribute to the Partnership all the net
proceeds and property (if any) received by SSG with respect to such Capital </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">16 </P>

</DIV></Center>

<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">
Stock. Upon the contribution by SSG to the Partnership of all (but not less than all) of such net proceeds and property (if any) so received by SSG, the General Partner shall cause the
Partnership to issue a number of Equivalent Units equal to the number of shares of Capital Stock so issued, registered in the name of SSG, such that, at all times, the number of relevant class of Equivalent Units held by SSG equals the number of
outstanding shares of the relevant class of Capital Stock. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:5%; text-indent:11%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">(e)&#8195;If, at any time, any shares of
Capital Stock are repurchased (whether by exercise of a put or call, pursuant to an open market purchase, automatically or by means of another arrangement) by SSG for cash or other consideration, then the General Partner shall cause the Partnership,
immediately prior to such repurchase of such Capital Stock, to redeem an equal number of Equivalent Units held by SSG, at an aggregate redemption price equal to the aggregate purchase price of the Capital Stock being repurchased by SSG (plus any
expenses related thereto) and upon such other terms as are the same for the Capital Stock being cancelled or retired by SSG. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:5%; text-indent:11%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">(f)&#8195;Any subdivision (by stock split, stock dividend, reclassification, recapitalization or otherwise)
or combination (by reverse stock split, reclassification, recapitalization or otherwise) of a class of Capital Stock shall be accompanied by an identical subdivision or combination of the Equivalent Units to maintain at all times a <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">one-to-one</FONT></FONT> ratio between the number of Equivalent Units and the number of outstanding shares of the applicable class of Capital Stock. Any corrective action to maintain such
ratios shall not be subject to a corresponding adjustment that would render the corrective action ineffective. In the implementation and administration of this <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;3.3.4</U>, the General Partner shall have authority to
amend this Agreement without the consent of any Limited Partner and shall have discretion to make such adjustments as it determines in good faith to be appropriate to reflect the economic equivalency intended hereby. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">3.3.5&#8195;<U>Class B2 Units</U>. The Partnership has established the Class&nbsp;B2 Units which were issued to Active
Partners as compensation for services rendered or to be rendered to or for the benefit of the Partnership or its Affiliates. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:5%; text-indent:11%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">(a)&#8195;The Class&nbsp;B2 Units are subject to the limitations on distributions contained in <U>Sections
4.3</U> and <U>4.4</U>. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:5%; text-indent:11%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">(b)&#8195;Each Class&nbsp;B2 Limited Partner shall have an initial Base
Percentage Interest with respect to its Class&nbsp;B2 Units of zero percent (0%) and such Base Percentage Interest shall increase as its Class&nbsp;B2 Units vest in accordance with <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;7.11.1</U>; <I>provided</I>, that for
the avoidance of doubt, for purposes of <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;4.1</U> and <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;4.7</U>, a Class&nbsp;B2 Limited Partner&#146;s Base Percentage Interest shall be zero percent (0%) with respect to any Class&nbsp;B2
Units (and shall not be entitled to any distributions in respect of any of its Class&nbsp;B2 Units under such Sections) until the Full Vesting Date of such Class&nbsp;B2 Units. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:5%; text-indent:11%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">(c)&#8195;Upon a Termination Event with respect to a Class&nbsp;B2 Limited Partner, such Class&nbsp;B2
Limited Partner&#146;s Class&nbsp;B2 Units shall be treated in accordance with <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;7.11</U>. </P>
