<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:5%; text-indent:11%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">(d)&#8195;No Class&nbsp;B2 Unit shall confer on the holder
any right to vote or consent on any matter arising under this Agreement prior to the Full Vesting Date of such Class&nbsp;B2 Unit. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:5%; text-indent:11%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">(e)&#8195;<U>Treatment of Class</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;B2 as Class</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;B Units</U>. Class&nbsp;B2
Units shall be treated as, and shall automatically be redesignated as, Class&nbsp;B Units from and after the later to occur of (i)&nbsp;the Full Vesting Date and (ii)&nbsp;the time at which the Capital Account balance attributable to such
Class&nbsp;B2 Units equals the Target Balance with respect to such Class&nbsp;B2 Units. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:5%; text-indent:11%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">(f)&#8195;<U>Intended Tax Treatment of Class</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;B2 Units</U>. The Class&nbsp;B2 Units are
intended to be treated for tax purposes as &#147;profits interests&#148; within the meaning of Rev. Proc. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">93-27,</FONT> <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">1993-2</FONT> C.B. 343, and Rev. Proc. <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2001-43,</FONT> <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2001-2</FONT> C.B. 191. The receipt of the Class&nbsp;B2 Units is intended to be treated as a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-taxable</FONT> event for the Partnership
and the holder. Each holder of Class&nbsp;B2 Units agrees not to take any position inconsistent with the foregoing. The Partnership and the Partners shall treat each holder of Class&nbsp;B2 Units as a partner for U.S. federal income tax purposes as
of the grant date of such holder&#146;s Class&nbsp;B2 Units. Each holder of Class&nbsp;B2 Units shall take into account the distributive share of the Partnership&#146;s income, gain, loss, deduction, and credit associated with its Class&nbsp;B2
Units in computing such holder&#146;s income tax liability for the entire period during which such Person holds the Class&nbsp;B2 Units. Upon the grant of the Class&nbsp;B2 Units or at the time the Class&nbsp;B2 Units become substantially vested,
neither the Partnership nor any of the Partners shall deduct any amount (as wages, compensation, or otherwise) for the fair market value of the Class&nbsp;B2 Units. No holder of Class&nbsp;B2 Units shall dispose of any Class&nbsp;B2 Units within two
years of receipt without the express prior written consent of the General Partner. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:5%; text-indent:11%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">(g)&#8195;<U>Election
Under Code Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;83(b)</U>. Absent a contrary determination by the General Partner, each holder of Class&nbsp;B2 Units shall file a valid and timely election pursuant to Code section 83(b) with respect to its Class&nbsp;B2 Units
and provide a copy of the election to the General Partner within thirty (30)&nbsp;days after issuance of the Class&nbsp;B2 Units. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:5%; text-indent:11%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">(h)&#8195;<U>Proposed Safe Harbor Election</U>. Each holder of Class&nbsp;B2 Units authorizes the Partnership
to make the safe harbor election provided for by the Revenue Procedure proposed in Notice <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2005-43,</FONT> <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2005-2</FONT> C.B. 107, or any similar election provided in published
guidance relating to the compensatory transfer of partnership interests (in any case, a &#147;<B>Safe Harbor Election</B>&#148;) in the manner that the General Partner determines will be most advantageous to the Partnership. Each such holder agrees
to cooperate with the Partnership to perfect and maintain any Safe Harbor Election and to timely execute and deliver any documentation with respect thereto reasonably requested by the General Partner. Each of the Partnership and each such holder
agrees to comply with all requirements of the Safe Harbor Election. A Safe Harbor Election once made may be revoked by the Partnership if permitted by the rules applicable to the Safe Harbor Election. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">3.3.6&#8195;<U>SPD Investors</U>. The Partnership issued Partnership Interests to SCP, which Partnership Interests
were&nbsp;redesignated as Class&nbsp;B Units. It is understood that SCP is a holding vehicle for the SCP Partners and it is agreed that for </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">18 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">
certain limited purposes set forth in this <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;3.3.6</U> SCP will be treated as holding separate Class&nbsp;B Units corresponding to the economic interests of the SCP
Partners in SCP. The provisions of this Agreement will be applied and interpreted in accordance with the following principles: </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:5%; text-indent:11%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">(a)&#8195;The provisions of <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;3.5</U> shall not apply to the Class&nbsp;B Units
held by SCP. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:5%; text-indent:11%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">(b)&#8195;The provisions of <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;7.1</U> shall not apply to
transfers of interests in SCP to the SCP Partners. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:5%; text-indent:11%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">(c)&#8195;The Class&nbsp;B Units held by SCP are not
subject to reduction under the vesting provisions of <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;7.10.1</U>. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">3.4&#8195;<U>Additional
Limited Partners</U>. Subject to Section&nbsp;3.3.4, the General Partner is hereby authorized to issue interests in the Partnership and to admit one or more recipients of such interests as additional Limited Partners (&#147;<B>Additional Limited
Partners</B>&#148;) from time to time, on such terms and conditions as the General Partner may determine; <I>provided</I> that the General Partner shall have determined before such admission that such admission will not create a material risk that
the Partnership would become a &#147;publicly traded partnership&#148; (as such term is defined in Code sections 469(k)(2) or 7704(b)). As a condition to being admitted to the Partnership, each Additional Limited Partner shall execute an Admission
Agreement and such other instruments as the General Partner may determine. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">3.5&#8195;<U>Irrevocable Proxy</U>. Each
Active Partner, Class&nbsp;C Limited Partner and Class&nbsp;D Limited Partner hereby irrevocably grants to, and appoints, the General Partner as its exclusive proxy and
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">attorney-in-fact</FONT></FONT> with full power of substitution and resubstitution, for and in the name, place and stead of such Partner, to the full extent of such Partner&#146;s
voting and other rights with respect to all such Partner&#146;s Units, which proxy is irrevocable and which appointment is coupled with an interest, including for purposes of the Act, to vote, and to execute written consents with respect to, all
such Partner&#146;s Units on any matter arising under this Agreement. Each Active Partner, Class&nbsp;C Limited Partner and Class&nbsp;D Limited Partner hereby ratifies and confirms all that such irrevocable proxy may lawfully do or cause to be done
by virtue hereof (the &#147;<B>Proxy</B>&#148;). Each Active Partner, Class&nbsp;C Limited Partner and Class&nbsp;D Limited Partner agrees to execute any further agreement or form reasonably necessary or appropriate to confirm and effectuate the
grant of the Proxy contained herein. The Proxy shall bind the heirs, successors and assigns of the Active Partner, Class&nbsp;C Limited Partner and Class&nbsp;D Limited Partner. The General Partner agrees that it shall not take any action to
exercise the Proxy granted by any Active Partner unless and until the earlier of (i)&nbsp;the Termination Date with respect to such Active Partner or (ii)&nbsp;any purported Transfer of any Units or rights with respect thereto by such Active Partner
(whether voluntary or involuntary, including pursuant to Death, Incapacity or divorce) unless such Transfer has been approved by the General Partner and the Assignee has been admitted as a Substitute Partner in accordance with this Agreement. The
General Partner agrees that it shall not take any action to exercise the Proxy granted by any Class&nbsp;C Limited Partner or any Class&nbsp;D Limited Partner unless and until any purported Transfer of any Units or rights with respect thereto by
such Class&nbsp;C Limited Partner or any Class&nbsp;D Limited Partner (whether voluntary or involuntary, including pursuant to Death, Incapacity or divorce) has been approved by the General Partner and the Assignee has been admitted as a Substitute
Partner in accordance with this Agreement. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">19 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">3.6&#8195;<U>Partner Capital</U>. Except as otherwise provided in this
Agreement: (a)&nbsp;no Partner shall demand or be entitled to receive a return of or interest on its Capital Contributions or Capital Account and (b)&nbsp;no Partner shall withdraw any portion of its Capital Contributions or receive any
distributions from the Partnership as a return of capital on account of such Capital Contributions. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">3.7&#8195;<U>Partner
Loans</U>. No Limited Partner (other than SSG) shall be required or permitted to make any loans or otherwise lend any funds to the Partnership. No loans made by any Limited Partner to the Partnership shall have any effect on such Limited
Partner&#146;s Base Percentage Interest, such loans representing a debt of the Partnership payable or collectible solely from the assets of the Partnership in accordance with the terms and conditions upon which such loans were made. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">3.8&#8195;<U>Liability of Limited Partners</U>. Except as otherwise (i)&nbsp;required by any
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-waivable</FONT> provision of the Act or other applicable Law or (ii)&nbsp;provided herein: (a)&nbsp;no Limited Partner shall be personally liable in any manner whatsoever for any debt, liability or other
obligation of the Partnership, whether such debt, liability or other obligation arises in contract, tort, or otherwise; and (b)&nbsp;subject to Section&nbsp;4.7.2 and Section&nbsp;3.3.4, no Limited Partner shall in any event have any liability
whatsoever in excess of (i)&nbsp;the amount of its Capital Contributions, (ii)&nbsp;without duplication, its share of any assets and undistributed profits of the Partnership, and (iii)&nbsp;the amount of any wrongful distribution to such Limited
Partner, if, and only to the extent, such Limited Partner has actual knowledge (at the time of the distribution) that such distribution is made in violation of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Section&nbsp;18-607</FONT> of the Act. To the fullest
extent permitted by law, no Limited Partner shall have any liability to any other Limited Partner or former Limited Partner, for making any discretionary decisions under this Agreement, or casting any vote for (or refraining from voting) in
connection with the business and affairs of the Partnership. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>ARTICLE 4 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>DISTRIBUTIONS </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">4.1&#8195;<U>General Distributions</U>. Except as otherwise provided in this <U>Article 4</U>, <U>Article 8</U> or in any
applicable Class&nbsp;Designation, the General Partner shall determine the timing and amount of all distributions. Subject to the terms of any applicable Class&nbsp;Designation and the other provisions of this <U>Article 4</U>, any distributions
(including Tax Distributions, except to the extent provided in <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;4.2.4</U>) shall be made <I>pro rata</I> in accordance with their Base Percentage Interests. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">4.2&#8195;<U>Tax Distributions</U>. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">4.2.1&#8195;<U>Amount, Timing, and Treatment of Tax Distribution</U>. Notwithstanding any provision of
<U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;4.1</U> to the contrary, but subject to <U>Section&nbsp;4.2.4</U>, the Partnership shall distribute to the Partners <I>pro rata</I> in accordance with their Base Percentage Interests an amount of cash such that each
Partner receives distributions of cash (including those made pursuant to <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;4.1</U>) in respect of each Fiscal Year in an amount not less than the Partner&#146;s Assumed Tax Liability for such Fiscal Year (that
distribution, a &#147;<B>Tax Distribution</B>&#148;). Any Tax Distribution made to a Partner under this <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;4.2.1</U> shall be treated as an advance against, and shall reduce, future amounts due to such Partner under
<U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;4.1</U>. For purposes of this <U>Article 4</U>, guaranteed payments for services (within the meaning of Code section 707(c)) shall not be treated as distributions. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">20 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">4.2.2&#8195;<U>Calculation of Assumed Tax Liability</U>. For purposes of
calculating the amount of each Partner&#146;s Tax <I>Distribution</I> under <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;4.2.2</U>, a Partner&#146;s &#147;<B>Assumed Tax Liability</B>&#148; means an amount equal to the product of: </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:5%; text-indent:11%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">(a)&#8195;the sum of (i)&nbsp;the net taxable income and gain allocated to that Partner in the Fiscal Year
and (ii)&nbsp;to the extent (x)&nbsp;determined by the General Partner in its sole discretion and (y)&nbsp;attributable to the Partnership, the amount the Partner is required to include in income by reason of Code sections 707(c) (but not including
guaranteed payments for services within the meaning of Code section 707(c)), 951(a), and 951A(a); <I>multiplied by</I> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:5%; text-indent:11%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">(b)&#8195;the highest combined effective U.S. federal, state, and local marginal rate of tax applicable to an
individual resident in San Francisco, California or New York, New York (whichever is higher), or such higher assumed tax rate as determined by the General Partner, for the Fiscal Year (such tax rate, the &#147;<B>Assumed Tax Rate</B>&#148;). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">The calculation required by this <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;4.2.2</U> shall be made (i)&nbsp;taking into account
(w)&nbsp;the character of the income or gain and (x)&nbsp;any limitations on, or the availability of, deductions and net operating losses, and (ii)&nbsp;disregarding (y)&nbsp;the effect of any special basis adjustments under Code section 743(b) and
(z)&nbsp;the effect of the allocations required under Code section 704(c)(1)(A). </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:11%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">4.2.3&#8195;<U>Timing of Tax
Distributions</U>. If reasonably practicable, the Partnership shall make distributions of the estimated Tax Distributions in respect of a Fiscal Year on a quarterly basis to facilitate the payment of quarterly estimated income taxes, taking into
account amounts previously <I>distributed</I> by reason of this <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;4.2.3</U>. Not later than sixty (60)&nbsp;Business Days after the end of the Fiscal Year, the Partnership shall make a final Tax Distribution in an amount
sufficient to fulfill the Partnership&#146;s obligations under <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;4.2.1</U>. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">4.2.4&#8195;<U>Impact of Insufficient Cash Available for Distribution</U>. If the amount of Tax Distributions to be made
exceeds the amount of the cash available for distribution (taking into account any entity-level tax obligations or payments, including any related interest, penalties, or other costs), SSG shall receive the full amount of its Tax Distribution (but
calculated by substituting the words &#147;a corporation doing business&#148; for &#147;an individual resident&#148; in the definition of &#147;<B>Assumed Tax Rate</B>&#148;) before the other Partners receive any distribution under this
<U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;4.2</U>. The balance, if any, of cash available for distribution shall be distributed: </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:5%; text-indent:11%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">(a)&#8195;First, to the Partners (other than SSG) <I>pro rata</I> in accordance with their Base Percentage
Interests in an amount such that each such Partner has received distributions pursuant to this <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;4.2.4(a)</U> not less than their Assumed Tax Liability (calculated by substituting the words &#147;a corporation doing
business&#148; for &#147;an individual resident&#148; in the definition of &#147;<B>Assumed Tax Rate</B>&#148;); and </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:5%; text-indent:11%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">(b)&#8195;Thereafter, the balance, if any, to the Partners (including SSG) <I>pro rata</I> in accordance with
their Base Percentage Interests until each Partner has received the full amount of its Tax Distribution calculated in accordance with <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;4.2.2</U>. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">21 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">4.2.5&#8195;<U>No Tax Distributions on Liquidation</U>. No Tax Distributions
shall be made in connection with the liquidation of the Partnership. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">4.2.6&#8195;<U>Compensation for Services and
Self-Employment Tax Make-Whole Payments</U>. The Partners acknowledge that certain Active Partners (including former Active Partners), the Class&nbsp;C Limited Partners and the Class&nbsp;D Limited Partners will receive compensation for services,
and such compensation may, for U.S. federal income tax purposes, be treated as a guaranteed payment for services under Code section 707(c). For the avoidance of doubt, the Partnership may, but is not required to, pay any Partner an amount such that,
on an <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax</FONT> basis, the Partner receives the amount he or she would have received if the Partner had not been subject to self-employment tax by reason of the Partner&#146;s ownership of Units in the
Partnership (and instead had received his or her compensation as an employee for tax purposes). Notwithstanding anything to the contrary in this Agreement, any compensation or payments described in the two preceding sentences shall be treated as
guaranteed payments for services within the meaning of Code section 707(c) and shall not be treated as distributions under this <U>Article 4</U>. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">4.3&#8195;<U>Limitation on Distributions in Respect of Profits Units</U>. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">4.3.1&#8195;<U>No Distributions in Respect of Unvested Profits Interests</U>. No Class&nbsp;B2 Limited Partner shall be
<I>entitled</I> to participate in any distributions pursuant to <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;4.1</U> in respect of any of its Class&nbsp;B2 Units prior to the Full Vesting Date of such Class&nbsp;B2 Units (and then shall be entitled to participate
in distributions only in respect of any fiscal quarter commencing after the Full Vesting Date). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">4.3.2&#8195;<U>Limitations on Distributions in Respect of Class</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;B2 Units</U>. The Partnership shall not
make any distribution in respect of a Class&nbsp;B2 Unit to the extent that the General Partner determines that such distribution would (a)&nbsp;cause the Class&nbsp;B2 Unit to fail to qualify as profits interests (as that term is <I>used</I> in
<U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;3.3.5</U>) or (b)&nbsp;cause an allocation of income or gain (other than Intangible Asset Gain) in respect of a Class&nbsp;B2 Unit that is disproportionate to the amount that would be distributed in respect of such
Class&nbsp;B2 Unit but for this <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;4.3.2</U>. For the avoidance of doubt, the limitations on distributions imposed by this <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;4.3.2</U> shall not apply to any holder of a Class&nbsp;B2 Unit that
has a Capital Account balance at least equal to the relevant Target Balance. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">4.3.3&#8195;<U>Continued Right to Tax
Distributions</U><I>. </I>For the avoidance of doubt, this <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;4.3</U> shall not <I>alter</I> the Profits Unit Holder&#146;s right to Tax Distributions under <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;4.2</U>. Notwithstanding the other
provisions of this Agreement, such Tax Distributions shall be calculated and made by the Partnership by treating all Unvested Class&nbsp;B2 Units as if they were &#147;<B>substantially vested</B>&#148; within the meaning of Treas. Reg. &#167; <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">1.83-3(b).</FONT> </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">4.4&#8195;<U>Distributions of Class</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;B2 Dilution
Reserve</U>. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">4.4.1&#8195;Notwithstanding the provisions of <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;4.1</U> or
<U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;4.2</U>, the Partners hereby acknowledge and agree that the Class&nbsp;B2 Dilution Reserve shall be distributed as set forth in this <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;4.4</U>. <I>The</I> General Partner shall maintain a
schedule of persons entitled to distributions thereof and their respective potential shares of any distribution with respect to the Class&nbsp;B2 Dilution Reserve. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">22 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">4.4.2&#8195;The General Partner shall calculate, at least annually, the
number of Class&nbsp;B2 Units that have vested since the prior determination (the &#147;<B>Class</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;B2 Vesting Amount</B>&#148;), the number of Class&nbsp;B2 Units that have been forfeited since the prior determination (the
&#147;<B>Class</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;B2 Forfeiture Amount</B>&#148;) and the number of Class&nbsp;B2 Units outstanding at time of the prior determination (or, if no <I>determination</I> has been made, as of August&nbsp;19, 2019) (the &#147;<B>Initial
Class</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;B2 Amount</B>&#148;). Promptly after each such determination, a distribution shall be made from the Class&nbsp;B2 Dilution Reserve equal to (a)&nbsp;the ratio of the Class&nbsp;B2 Forfeiture Amount to the Initial
Class&nbsp;B2 Amount, multiplied by (b)&nbsp;the Class&nbsp;B2 Dilution Reserve, to the 2019 Redeemed Partners pro rata based on the number of Units redeemed from each 2019 Redeemed Partner in the 2019 Equity Transaction. Promptly after each such
determination, a distribution shall be made from the Class&nbsp;B2 Dilution Reserve equal to (a)&nbsp;the ratio of the Class&nbsp;B2 Vesting Amount to the Initial Class&nbsp;B2 Amount, multiplied by (b)&nbsp;the Class&nbsp;B2 Dilution Reserve, to
the Limited Partners holding 2019 Dilutable Units, pro rata based on the number of 2019 Dilutable Units held by them at such time. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">4.5&#8195;<U>Distributions Upon Liquidation</U>. Distributions made in conjunction with the final liquidation of the
Partnership shall be applied or distributed as provided in <U>Article 8</U>. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">4.6&#8195;<U>Distributions to Reflect
Additional Units</U>. If the Partnership issues additional Units, subject to the terms of any applicable Class&nbsp;Designation, the General Partner is authorized to make such revisions to this <U>Article 4</U> and to <U>Article 5</U> as it
determines are reasonably necessary or desirable to reflect the issuance of such additional Units, including making preferential distributions to certain classes of Units. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">4.7&#8195;<U>Other Distribution Rules</U>. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">4.7.1&#8195;<U>Record Date for Distributions</U>. The Partnership may designate a Distribution Record Date for purposes of
calculating and giving effect to distributions. All distributions attributable to a Unit with respect to which the Distribution Record Date is before the date of any Transfer shall be made to the transferor Partner or the tendering Partner (as the
case may be) and, in the case of a Transfer other than an exchange pursuant to the Class&nbsp;B Exchange Agreement, the Class&nbsp;C Exchange Agreement or the Class&nbsp;D Exchange Agreement, all distributions thereafter attributable to such Unit
shall be made to the transferee Partner. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">4.7.2&#8195;<U>Over-Distributions</U>. If the Partnership distributes to a
Partner more than the amount to which the Partner in entitled (e.g., by reason of an accounting error), the Partner shall, upon written notice of the over-distribution delivered to the Partner within one year of the over-distribution, promptly
return the over-distribution to the Partnership. For the avoidance of doubt, this <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;4.7.2</U> applies to any distribution made under this Agreement. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">4.7.3&#8195;<U>Reimbursements of Preformation Capital Expenditures</U>. To the extent a distribution (or reduction in a
Partner&#146;s share of Partnership liabilities for federal tax purposes) would otherwise be treated as proceeds in a sale under Code section&nbsp;707(a)(2)(B), the Partners intend such actual or deemed distribution to reimburse preformation capital
expenditures under Treas. Reg. &#167; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">1.707-4(d)</FONT> to the maximum extent permitted by Law. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">23 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">4.8&#8195;<U>Distributions in Kind</U>. No right is given to any Partner to
demand or receive property other than cash as provided in this Agreement. The General Partner may make a distribution in kind of Partnership assets to the Partners, and such Partnership assets shall be distributed in such a fashion as to ensure that
the fair market value (as determined in good faith by the General Partner) thereof is distributed and allocated in accordance with this <U>Article 4</U> and <U>Article 5</U> and <U>Article 8</U>. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">4.9&#8195;<U>Limitations on Distributions</U>. Notwithstanding any provision to the contrary contained in this Agreement,
neither the Partnership nor the General Partner, on behalf of the Partnership, shall make a distribution to any Partner on account of its Partnership Interests in violation of the Act or other applicable Law or to the extent such distribution would
result in the Partnership or any of its Subsidiaries being in default under any material credit agreement, loan agreement, note, indenture or other agreement governing indebtedness. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>ARTICLE 5 </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>ALLOCATIONS
OF NET PROFITS AND NET LOSSES </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">5.1&#8195;<U>Allocation Generally</U>. Each Fiscal Year, after adjusting each
Partner&#146;s Capital Account for all contributions and distributions with respect to such Fiscal Year and after giving effect to the allocations under <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;5.2</U> for the Fiscal Year, Net Profits and Net Losses (or items
thereof) of the Partnership shall be allocated among the Partners in a manner such that, after such allocations have been made, each Partner&#146;s Capital Account balance (which may be a positive, negative, or zero balance) will equal
(proportionately)&nbsp;(a) the amount that would be distributed to each such Partner, determined as if the Partnership were to (i)&nbsp;sell all of its assets for their Gross Asset Values, (ii)&nbsp;satisfy all of its liabilities in accordance with
their terms with the proceeds from such sale (limited, with respect to nonrecourse liabilities, to the Gross Asset Values of the assets securing such liabilities), and (iii)&nbsp;distribute the remaining proceeds pursuant to
<U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;4.1</U> minus (b)&nbsp;the sum of (x)&nbsp;such Partner&#146;s Partnership Minimum Gain and Partner Nonrecourse Debt Minimum Gain and (y)&nbsp;the amount, if any (without duplication of any amount included under clause
(x)), that such Partner is obligated (or is deemed for U.S. federal income tax purposes to be obligated) to contribute, in its capacity as a Partner, to the capital of the Partnership as of the last day of such Fiscal Year. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">5.2&#8195;<U>Priority Allocations</U>. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">5.2.1&#8195;<U>Partnership Minimum Gain Chargeback</U>. Except as otherwise provided in Treas. Reg. &#167; <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">1.704-2(f),</FONT> if there is a net decrease in Partnership Minimum Gain during any Fiscal Year, each Partner shall be specially allocated items of Partnership income and gain for such Fiscal Year (and, if necessary,
subsequent Fiscal Years) in proportion to, and to the extent of, an amount equal to the portion of such Partner&#146;s share of the net decrease in Partnership Minimum Gain, determined in accordance with Treas. Reg. &#167; <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">1.704-2(g).</FONT> This <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;5.2.1</U> is intended to comply with the minimum gain chargeback requirement in Treas. Reg. &#167; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">1.704-2(f)</FONT> and shall be
interpreted consistently therewith. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">5.2.2&#8195;<U>Partner Nonrecourse Debt Minimum Gain Chargeback</U>. Except as
otherwise provided in Treas. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Reg.&nbsp;&#167;&nbsp;1.704-2(i)(4),</FONT> notwithstanding any other provision of this <U>Article 5</U>, if there is a net decrease in Partner Nonrecourse Debt Minimum Gain attributable
to Partner Nonrecourse Debt during any taxable year, then each Partner who has a share of </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">24 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">
the Partner Nonrecourse Debt Minimum Gain attributable to such Partner Nonrecourse Debt, determined in accordance with Treas. Reg. &#167; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">1.704-2(i)(5),</FONT>
shall be specially allocated items of Partnership income and gain for such Fiscal Year (and, if necessary, subsequent Fiscal Years) in an amount equal to such Partner&#146;s share of the net decrease in Partner Nonrecourse Debt, determined in
accordance with Treas. Reg. &#167; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">1.704-2(i)(4).</FONT> This <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;5.2.2</U> is intended to comply with the minimum gain chargeback requirement in Treas. Reg.
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">&#167;&nbsp;1.704-2(i)</FONT> and shall be interpreted consistently therewith. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">5.2.3&#8195;<U>Qualified Income Offset</U>. If any Partner unexpectedly receives an adjustment, allocation or distribution
described in Treas. Reg. &#167; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">1.704-1(b)(2)(ii)(d)(4),</FONT> (5) or (6), items of Partnership income and gain shall be allocated, in accordance with Treas. Reg. &#167;
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">1.704-1(b)(2)(ii)(d),</FONT> to such Partner in an amount and manner sufficient to eliminate, to the extent required by such Regulations, the Adjusted Capital Account Deficit of such Partner as quickly as possible,
provided that an allocation pursuant to this <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;5.2.3</U> shall be made if and only to the extent that such Partner would have an Adjusted Capital Account Deficit after all other allocations provided in this <U>Article
5</U> have been tentatively made as if this <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;5.2.3</U> were not in the Agreement. It is intended that this <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;5.2.3</U> comply with the qualified income offset requirement in Treas. Reg. &#167;
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">1.704-1(b)(2)(ii)(d)</FONT> and shall be interpreted consistently therewith. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">5.2.4&#8195;<U>Gross Income Allocation</U>. In the event that any Partner has a deficit Capital Account at the end of any
Fiscal Year that is in excess of the sum of (A)&nbsp;the amount (if any) that such Partner is obligated to restore to the Partnership upon complete liquidation of such Partner&#146;s Partnership Interest and (B)&nbsp;the amount that such Partner is
deemed to be obligated to restore pursuant to the penultimate sentences of Treas. Reg. &#167;&#167; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">1.704-2</FONT> (g)(1) and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">1.704-2(i)(5),</FONT> each such Partner shall be
specially allocated items of Partnership income and gain in the amount of such excess to eliminate such deficit as quickly as possible, provided that an allocation pursuant to this <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;5.2.4</U> shall be made if and only to
the extent that such Partner would have a deficit Capital Account in excess of such sum after all other allocations provided in this <U>Article 5</U> have been tentatively made as if this <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;5.2.4</U> and
<U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;5.2.3</U> were not in the Agreement. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">5.2.5&#8195;<U>Nonrecourse Deductions</U>. Nonrecourse
Deductions for any Fiscal Year shall be allocated to the Partners in proportion to Units, unless otherwise determined by the General Partner. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">5.2.6&#8195;<U>Partner Nonrecourse Deductions</U>. Any Partner Nonrecourse Deductions for any Fiscal Year shall be specially
allocated to the Partner who bears the economic risk of loss (within the meaning of Treas. Reg. &#167; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">1.752-2)</FONT> with respect to the Partner Nonrecourse Liability to which such Partner Nonrecourse Deductions
are attributable in accordance with Treas. Reg. &#167; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">1.704-2(i)(l).</FONT> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">5.2.7&#8195;<U>Special Basis Adjustments</U>. To the extent that an adjustment to the adjusted tax basis of any Partnership
asset pursuant to Code section 734(b) or Code section 743(b) is required, pursuant to Treas. Reg. &#167; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">1.704-1(b)(2)(iv)(m)(2)</FONT> or&nbsp;Treas. Reg. &#167;
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">1.704-1(b)(2)(iv)(m)(4),</FONT> to be taken into account in determining Capital Accounts as the result of a distribution to a holder of Units in complete liquidation of its interest in the Partnership, the amount of
such adjustment to the Capital Accounts shall be treated as an item of gain (if the adjustment increases the basis of the asset) or loss (if the adjustment </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">25 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">
decreases such basis), and such gain or loss shall be specially allocated to the holders of Units in accordance with their respective Base Percentage Interests in the event that Treas. Reg. <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">&#167;&nbsp;1.704-1(b)(2)(iv)(m)(2)</FONT> applies, or to the Partner(s) to whom such distribution was made in the event that Treas. Reg. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">&#167;&nbsp;1.704-1(b)(2)(iv)(m)(4)</FONT> applies.
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">5.2.8&#8195;<U>Limitation on Allocation of Net Losses</U>. No allocation of Net Losses (or items of loss) shall be
allocated to a Partner to the extent that any such allocation would cause or increase an Adjusted Capital Account Deficit as to the Partner. The limitation set forth in the preceding sentence shall be applied on a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Partner-by-Partner</FONT></FONT> basis and Net Losses (or items of loss) not allocable to a Partner as a result of such limitation shall be reallocated (A)&nbsp;first, among the other holders of Units in accordance with
their respective Base Percentage Interests, and (B)&nbsp;thereafter, among the holders of other Units, as determined by the Partnership, in each case subject to the limitations of this <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;5.2.8</U>. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">5.2.9&#8195;<U>Ameliorative Allocations</U>. Any allocations made pursuant to <U>Sections 5.2.1</U> through 5.2.8
(collectively, the &#147;<B>Regulatory Allocations</B>&#148;) shall be taken into account in allocating other items of income, gain, loss and deduction among the holders of Units so that to the extent possible without violating the requirements
giving rise to the Regulatory Allocations, the net amount of such allocations of other items and the Regulatory Allocations to each holder of a Unit shall be equal to the net amount that would have been allocated to each such Partner if the
Regulatory Allocations had not occurred. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">5.2.10&#8195;<U>Intangible Asset Gain</U>. Intangible Asset Gain shall be
allocated to each holder of Class&nbsp;B2 Units so as to cause the Capital Account balance of such Limited Partner (to the extent attributable to its Class&nbsp;B2 Units) to stand in the same ratio to the aggregate Capital Account balances
attributable to all holders of Units as the number of Class&nbsp;B2 Units held by such holder bears to the total number of Units outstanding at the time of such allocation (such amount with respect to each such holder of Class&nbsp;B2 Units, the
&#147;<B>Target Balance</B>&#148;). To the extent there is insufficient Intangible Asset Gain to reach the Target Balance for each holder of Class&nbsp;B2 Units, Intangible Asset Gain shall be allocated in such manner as may be determined by the
General Partner. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">5.3&#8195;<U>Other Allocation Rules</U>. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">5.3.1&#8195;<U>In General</U>. Except as otherwise provided in this <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;5.3</U>, for income tax
purposes under the Code and the Regulations, each Partnership item of income, gain, loss, deduction, and credit (collectively, &#147;<B>Tax Items</B>&#148;) shall be allocated among the Partners in the same manner as its correlative item of income,
gain, loss, deduction, and credit (as calculated for purposes of allocating Net Profits or Net Losses, including items allocated under <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;5.2</U>) is allocated pursuant to <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;5.1</U> and
<U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;5.2</U>. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">5.3.2&#8195;<U>Section 704(c) Allocations</U>. Notwithstanding any provision of
<U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;5.3.1</U> to the contrary, in accordance with Code section 704(c)(1)(A) (and the principles of those provisions) and Treas. Reg. &#167; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">1.704-3,</FONT> Tax Items with respect to any
property contributed to the capital of the Partnership, or after Partnership has been revalued under Treas. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Reg.&nbsp;&#167;&nbsp;1.704-1(b)(2)(iv)(f)</FONT> or (s), shall, solely for United States federal, state and
local tax purposes, be allocated among the </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">26 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">
Partners so as to take into account any variation between the adjusted basis of such Partnership property to the Partnership for United States federal income tax purposes and its value as so
determined at the time of the contribution or revaluation of Partnership property. The Partnership shall account for such variation under the traditional method as described in Treas. Reg. &#167; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">1.704-3(b).</FONT>
For the avoidance of doubt, allocations pursuant to this <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;5.3.2</U> are solely for purposes of U.S. federal, state, and local taxes and shall not affect, or in any way be taken into account in computing, any
Partner&#146;s Capital Account or such Partner&#146;s share of Net Profits or Net Losses (or items thereof), or distributions under any provision of this Agreement. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">5.3.3&#8195;<U>Allocation of Excess Nonrecourse Liabilities</U>. For purposes of determining a Partner&#146;s share of the
&#147;excess nonrecourse liabilities&#148; of the Partnership within the meaning of Treas. Reg. &#167; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">1.752-3(a)(3),</FONT> each Partner&#146;s interest in Partnership profits shall equal such Partner&#146;s Base
Percentage Interest with respect to Units, or such other share as the General Partner determines. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">5.3.4&#8195;<U>Allocations in Respect of Varying Interests</U>. If any Partner&#146;s interest in the Partnership varies
(within the meaning of Code section 706(d)), whether by reason of a Transfer of a Unit, redemption of a Unit by the Partnership, or otherwise, Net Profits and Net Losses (and items thereof) for such Fiscal Year shall be allocated so as to take into
account such varying interests in accordance with Code section 706(d) using the &#147;interim closing of the books&#148; method and/or such other permissible method or methods selected by the General Partner. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">5.3.5&#8195;<U>Timing and Amount of Allocations of Net Profits and Net Losses</U>. Net Profits and Net Losses (or items
thereof) of the Partnership shall be determined and allocated with respect to each Fiscal Year as of the end of each such year, or at such other time or times determined by the General Partner. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">5.3.6&#8195;<U>Modification of Allocations</U>. The allocations set forth in <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;5.1</U> and
<U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;5.2</U> are intended to comply with certain requirements of the Regulations. Notwithstanding the other provisions of this <U>Article 5</U>, the General Partner shall be authorized to make, in its reasonable discretion,
appropriate amendments to the allocations of Net Profits and Net Losses (or items thereof) pursuant to this Agreement (i)&nbsp;in order to comply with Code section 704 or applicable Regulations or (ii)&nbsp;to allocate properly items of income,
gain, loss, deduction and credit to those Partners who bear the economic burden or benefit associated therewith. If there are any changes after the date of this Agreement in applicable tax Law, regulations or interpretation, or any errors,
ambiguities, inconsistencies or omissions in this Agreement with respect to allocations to be made to Capital Accounts that would, individually or in the aggregate, cause the Partners not to achieve the economic objectives underlying this Agreement,
the General Partner may in its discretion make appropriate adjustments to such allocations in order to achieve or approximate such economic objectives. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">5.4&#8195;<U>Preparation of Partnership Tax Returns</U>. The General Partner shall arrange for the preparation and timely
filing of all returns required of the Partnership for federal, state, and local income tax purposes. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">5.5&#8195;<U>No
Right to Review Partner Tax Returns</U>. With respect to the financial statements or tax returns of a Partner or its Affiliates, none of the Partnership, the General Partner, the other Partners, such other Partner&#146;s Affiliates or any of their
respective representatives, will be entitled to review such financial statements or tax returns for any purpose, including in connection with any proceeding or other dispute (whether involving the Partnership, between the Partners, or involving any
other Persons). </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">5.6&#8195;<U>No Inconsistent Positions</U>. Except as required by applicable Law or previously authorized
in writing by the Partnership, which authorization may be withheld in the sole discretion of the Partnership, no Partner shall (a)&nbsp;independently </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">27 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">
act with respect to tax audits or tax litigation affecting or arising from the Partnership, or (b)&nbsp;treat any Partnership item inconsistently on such Partner&#146;s income tax return with the
treatment of the item on the Partnership&#146;s tax return and/or the Schedule <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">K-1</FONT> (or other written information statement) provided to such Partner. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">5.7&#8195;<U>Tax Elections</U>. The Partnership shall have in effect (and shall cause each Subsidiary that is classified as a
partnership for U.S. federal income tax purposes to have in effect) an election pursuant to Code section 754 (and any similar provisions of applicable U.S. state or local law) for the Partnership for the Fiscal Year that includes the closing date of
SSG&#146;s initial public offering of shares of its Class&nbsp;A Common Stock and each Fiscal Year in which a sale, exchange, or redemption (whether partial or complete) occurs. This <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;5.7</U> shall not apply with respect
to any Subsidiary that the Partnership cannot cause to make a section 754 election, with respect to Subsidiaries that would not customarily make a section 754 election at the Partnership&#146;s request, or with respect to any other Subsidiary that
the General Partner determines is immaterial or otherwise insignificant. Except as otherwise provided in this Agreement, the General Partner shall determine whether to make any other available election pursuant to the Code. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">5.8&#8195;<U>Tax Representative</U>. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">5.8.1&#8195;Appointment of Tax Representative and Designated Individual. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:5%; text-indent:11%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">(a)&#8195;<U>Tax Representative</U>. The General Partner shall act as the Tax Representative, but the General
Partner may designate another Person to act as the Tax Representative and may remove, replace, or revoke the designation of that Person, or require that Person to resign. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:5%; text-indent:11%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">(b)&#8195;<U>Designated Individual</U>. If a Person that is not an individual is the Tax Representative, the
General Partner shall appoint a &#147;designated individual&#148; for each taxable year (as described in Treas. Reg. &#167; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">301.6223-1(b)(3)(ii))</FONT> (a &#147;<B>Designated Individual</B>&#148;). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">5.8.2&#8195;<U>Authority of the Tax Representative; Delegation of Authority</U>. The Tax Representative shall have all of the
rights, duties, powers, and obligations provided for under the Code, Regulations, or other applicable guidance; <I>provided</I>, <I>however</I>, that if a Person other than the General Partner is the Tax Representative, the Tax Representative shall
in all cases act solely at the direction of the General Partner. The Tax Representative may delegate its authority under this <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;5.8</U> to a Designated Individual; <I>provided</I>, for the avoidance of doubt, that each
Designated Individual shall in all cases act solely at the direction of the General Partner. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">5.8.3&#8195;<U>Costs and
Indemnification</U>. The Partnership shall pay, or to the extent the Tax Representative or Designated&nbsp;Individual pays, indemnify and reimburse, to the fullest extent permitted by applicable Law, the Tax Representative
</P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">28 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">
or Designated Individual, for all costs and expenses, including legal and accounting fees (as such fees are incurred) and any claims incurred in connection with any tax audit or judicial review
proceeding with respect to the tax liability of the Partnership. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">5.9&#8195;<U>Partnership Audits</U>. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">5.9.1&#8195;<U>Determinations with Respect to Audits</U>. The General Partner shall make all decisions and determinations with
respect to, and shall have sole authority with respect to the conduct of, audits of the Partnership, including whether to cause the Partnership or any Subsidiary to make a Push Out Election with respect to any adjustment that could result in an
imputed underpayment (within the meaning of Code section 6225) (an &#147;<B>Imputed Underpayment</B>&#148;). No Partner shall take any action or make any filing inconsistent with the actions of the Tax Representative or Designated Individual. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">5.9.2&#8195;<U>Imputed Underpayment Share</U>. To the extent the Partnership (or any Subsidiary that is classified as a
partnership for U.S. federal income tax purposes) is liable for any Imputed Underpayment, the General Partner shall determine the liability of the Partners for a share of such Imputed Underpayment, taking into account the Partner&#146;s Units and
the status and actions of the Partners (including any related interest, penalties or other costs, such share, an &#147;<B>Imputed Underpayment Share</B>&#148;). The General Partner shall cause each Partner to bear its Imputed Underpayment Share
solely by reducing the amount of distributions made to such Partner pursuant to <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;4.1</U> or <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;8.5.</U> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">5.10&#8195;<U>Information to be Provided by Partners to Partnership</U>. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:10%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">5.10.1&#8195;<U>Notice of Audit or Tax Examination</U>. Each Partner shall notify the Partnership within five days after
receipt of any notice regarding an audit or tax examination of the Partnership and upon any request for material information by United States federal, state, local, or other tax authorities. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:10%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">5.10.2&#8195;<U>Information Relating to FATCA</U>. Each Partner shall provide the Partnership with any information,
representations, certificates or forms relating to such Partner (or its direct or indirect owners or account holders) that are reasonably requested from time to time by the Partnership and that are necessary in&nbsp;order for the Partnership or any
entity in&nbsp;which the Partnership or holds (directly or indirectly) an interest (whether in the form of debt or equity) and any Partner of any &#147;expanded affiliated group&#148; (as defined in Code section 1471(e)(2)) to (i)&nbsp;enter into,
maintain or comply with any agreement required to be filed with the IRS as contemplated by Code section 1471(b), (ii) satisfy any requirement imposed under FATCA in order to avoid any withholding required under FATCA (including any withholding upon
any payments to such Partner under this Agreement) or (iii)&nbsp;comply with any information reporting or withholding requirements under FATCA. In addition, each Partner shall take such actions as the Tax Representative may reasonably request in
connection with the foregoing. If any Partner fails to provide any of the information, representations, certificates or forms (or undertake any of the actions) required under this <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;5.10.2</U> in a timely manner, the Tax
Representative shall have full authority to take any steps (after providing such Partner with written notice) that the Partnership determines in its reasonable discretion are necessary to comply with FATCA and to mitigate the effect on the
Partnership of such failure including, but not limited to, withholding on </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">29 </P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">
payments or distributions made to such Partner and requiring such Partner to transfer its Units or otherwise withdraw from the Partnership. If requested by the Partnership, such Partner shall
execute any and all documents, opinions, instruments and certificates to effectuate the foregoing. If a Partner fails to comply with the terms of this <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;5.10.2</U> and, as a result of such failure, any withholding tax is
imposed under FATCA on distributions to the Partnership, such Partner shall, unless otherwise agreed in writing by the Partnership, to the fullest extent permitted by applicable Law, indemnify and hold harmless the Partnership and its Affiliates for
all losses, costs, fees, expenses, damages, claims, and demands (including any withholding tax, penalties or interest suffered by the Partnership). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:1%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">5.10.3&#8195;<U>Other Information</U>. Each Partner shall provide to the Partnership upon request tax basis information about
assets contributed by it to the Partnership and such other tax information as reasonably requested by the Partnership and necessary for it to prepare its financial reports or any tax returns, or otherwise to comply with applicable Law. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">5.11&#8195;<U>Information to be Provided by Partnership to Partners</U>. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:10%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">5.11.1&#8195;<U>Communication with IRS</U>. The Partnership shall, within thirty (30)&nbsp;days after receipt, forward to
each Partner holding more than twenty percent (20%) of the Units a photocopy of any material correspondence relating to the Partnership received from the IRS and, within thirty (30)&nbsp;days after occurrence, advise each Partner in writing of the
substance of any material conversation affecting the Partnership held with any representative of the IRS. Notwithstanding the foregoing, the Partnership may withhold information from the Partners to the extent the Partnership determines that
providing such information could result in the waiver of any privilege or otherwise be harmful to the Partnership. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:10%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">5.11.2&#8195;<U>Notice of Tax Benefits</U>. The Partnership shall use its reasonable best efforts to deliver to each Partner
notice of any <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">tax-related</FONT> benefit (as reasonably determined by the Partnership) that any Partner may be able to claim with respect to taxes imposed on the Partnership or any investment, within a reasonable
period of time of the Partnership&#146;s becoming aware of that benefit. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">5.12&#8195;<U>Survival of Obligations</U>. For
purposes of this <U>Article 5</U>, the term &#147;<B>Partner</B>&#148; shall include a former Partner, except to the extent the General Partner determines that such inclusion is inconsistent with the intention that former Partners be liable for
their appropriate share of the Partnership&#146;s taxes. The rights and obligations of each Partner and former Partner under this <U>Article 5</U> shall survive the Transfer by such Partner of its Units (or withdrawal by a Partner or redemption of a
Partner&#146;s Units) and the dissolution of the Partnership until ninety (90)&nbsp;days after the applicable statute of limitations. <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;5.8</U>, <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;5.9</U>, and this
<U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;5.12</U> shall not be amended without the prior written consent of any Partner or former Partner that would be materially and adversely impacted by such amendment. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">5.13&#8195;<U>Withholding</U>. Each Partner acknowledges and agrees that the Partnership may be required by Law to deduct and
withhold taxes or to fulfill other similar obligations of such Partner on any amount paid, distributed, disbursed, or allocated by the Partnership to that Partner, including upon liquidation, and any assignee or transferee of a Partner&#146;s
interest or substituted </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">30 </P>

Partner shall, by reason of such transfer, assignment or substitution, acknowledge, and agree to any such withholding by the Partnership, including withholding to discharge obligations of the
Partnership with respect to prior distributions, allocations, or a Imputed Underpayment Share. All amounts withheld with respect to any allocation or distribution shall, except as otherwise provided in or determined by the Partnership pursuant to
<U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;5.9</U> be treated as amounts distributed to such Person pursuant to the provision of this Agreement that would have applied if such amount had actually been distributed. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">5.14&#8195;<U>Taxes Other Than U.S. Federal Income Taxes</U>. The provisions of this Agreement with respect to U.S. federal
income tax shall apply, <I>mutatis mutandis</I>, with respect to any similar provisions of state, local, or <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-U.S.</FONT> tax law as determined by the Partnership. References in
<U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;5.9</U>, <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;5.10</U>, <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;5.11</U>, <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;5.12</U>, and <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;5.13</U> to &#147;taxes&#148; shall include any
interest, penalties and additions to tax with respect to such taxes. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">5.15&#8195;<U>United States Person</U>. Other than
(i)&nbsp;persons who are Partners as of the date of this Agreement or (ii)&nbsp;Partners with respect to whom the General Partner has waived the application of this <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;5.15</U> in writing, each Partner represents and
covenants that, for U.S. federal income tax purposes, it is and will at all times remain a &#147;<B>United States person,</B>&#148; within the meaning of Code section 7701, or is and will at all times remain a disregarded entity the assets of which
are treated as owned by a United States person under Treas. Reg. &#167;&#167; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">301.7701-1,</FONT> <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">301.7701-2,</FONT> and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">301.7701-3.</FONT> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">5.16&#8195;<U>Tax Classification</U>. The Partnership shall be classified as a partnership for United States federal, state
and local tax purposes. Unless otherwise determined by the General Partner, the Subsidiaries of the Partnership shall be classified either as disregarded entities or as partnerships for United States federal, state and local tax purposes. No Person
shall take any action inconsistent with such classifications. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>ARTICLE 6 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>OPERATIONS </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">6.1&#8195;<U>Management Generally</U>. The management and control of the Partnership shall be vested exclusively in the
General Partner. Persons dealing with the Partnership are entitled to rely conclusively upon the power and authority of the General Partner as set forth herein. The Limited Partners shall have no part in the management or control of the Partnership
and shall have no authority or right to act on behalf of the Partnership or deal with third parties in connection with any matter. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">6.2&#8195;<U>Authority of and Approvals by the General Partner</U>. The General Partner shall have the power to do any and all
acts necessary or convenient to or for the furtherance of the purposes described herein, including all powers, statutory or otherwise, possessed by limited partnerships under the laws of the State of Delaware. Without limitation of the foregoing,
the General Partner is hereby authorized to execute, deliver and perform any document on behalf of the Partnership without any further act of any person or entity. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:5%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">6.3&#8195;<U>Duties, Exculpation and Indemnification</U>. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">31 </P>

<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">6.3.1&#8195;This Agreement is not intended to, and does not, create or
impose any fiduciary duty on any of the Partners (including, without limitation, the General Partner) hereto or on their respective Affiliates. Further, the Partners hereby waive any and all fiduciary duties that, absent such waiver, may exist at or
be implied by Law or in equity, and in doing so, recognize, acknowledge and agree that their duties and obligations to one another and to the Partnership are only as expressly set forth in this Agreement and those required by the Act. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">6.3.2&#8195;To the extent that, at law or in equity, any Partner (including, without limitation, the General Partner) has
duties (including fiduciary duties) and liabilities relating thereto to the Partnership or to another Partner, the Partners (including without limitation, the General Partner) acting under this Agreement will not be liable to the Partnership or to
any such other Partner for their good faith reliance on the provisions of this Agreement. The provisions of this Agreement, to the extent that they restrict or eliminate the duties and liabilities relating thereto of any Partner (including without
limitation, the General Partner) otherwise existing at law or in equity, are agreed by the Partners to replace to that extent such other duties and liabilities of the Partners relating thereto (including without limitation, the General Partner).
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">6.3.3&#8195;None of the General Partner, the Limited Partners, the Tax Representative, the Designated Individual or the
Affiliates, agents, officers, partners, employees, representatives, directors, members, managers or shareholders of the General Partner or the Partnership (collectively, the &#147;<B>Indemnitees</B>&#148;) shall be liable, responsible, or
accountable, in damages or otherwise, to the Partnership or any Partner thereof for doing any act or failing to do any act, the effect of which may cause or result in loss or damage to the Partnership or such Partner if: (a)&nbsp;the act or failure
to act of such Indemnitee was in good faith, within the scope of such Indemnitee&#146;s authority and in a manner it reasonably believed to be in, or not inconsistent with, the best interest of the Partnership, and (b)&nbsp;the conduct of such
Person did not constitute fraud, willful misconduct or gross negligence. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">6.3.4&#8195;Indemnitees shall be fully protected
in relying in good faith upon the records of the Partnership and upon such information, opinions, reports or statements presented to the Partnership by any Person as to matters the Indemnitee reasonably believes are within such other Person&#146;s
professional or expert competence and who has been selected with reasonable care by or on behalf of the Partnership, including information, opinions, reports or statements as to the value and amount of the assets, liabilities, profits, losses or
cash flow or any other facts pertinent to the existence or amount of assets from which distributions to Partners might properly be paid. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">6.3.5&#8195;The Partnership shall indemnify and hold harmless any Indemnitee to the greatest extent permitted by law against
any liability or loss as a result of any claim or legal proceeding by any Person (including by or through the Partnership and/or any Partner) relating to the performance or nonperformance of any act concerning the activities of the Partnership or in
furtherance of the Partnership&#146;s interests (including serving at the request of the Partnership as a director, officer, partner, trustee, employee or agent of another corporation, partnership, joint venture, trust, limited liability company,
nonprofit entity or other enterprise) if: (a)&nbsp;the act or failure to act of such Indemnitee was in good faith, within the scope of such Indemnitee&#146;s authority and in a manner it reasonably believed to be in the best interest of the
Partnership, and (b)&nbsp;the conduct of such Person did not constitute fraud, willful misconduct or gross negligence. The indemnification authorized by this <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;6.3.5</U> shall include any judgment, award, settlement, the
payment of reasonable attorneys&#146; fees and other expense incurred in settling or defending any claims, threatened action or finally adjudicated legal proceeding. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">32 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">6.3.6&#8195;From time to time, as requested by an Indemnitee, the
attorneys&#146; fees and other expenses described in <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;6.3.5</U> may, in the discretion of the General Partner, be advanced by the Partnership prior to the final disposition of such claims, actions or proceedings upon
receipt by the Partnership of an undertaking by or on behalf of such Indemnitee to repay such amounts if it shall be determined that such Indemnitee is not entitled to be indemnified as authorized hereunder. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">6.3.7&#8195;Any indemnification provided hereunder shall be satisfied solely out of the assets of the Partnership, as an
expense of the Partnership, unless otherwise determined by the General Partner. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">6.3.8&#8195;Notwithstanding anything in
this Agreement or any otherwise applicable provision of law or equity, whenever an Indemnitee is required or permitted to make a decision, take or approve an action, or omit to do any of the foregoing: (a)&nbsp;in its &#147;discretion&#148; or
&#147;sole discretion,&#148; under a similar grant of authority or latitude, or without an express standard of behavior (including, without limitation, standards such as &#147;reasonable&#148; or &#147;good faith&#148;), then such Indemnitee shall
